Paul \\\"P.J.\\\" Morton (\u0040pjmorton ) is an accomplished singer, songwriter, arranger, producer, author, multiple Grammy Award winner, and keyboardist who also plays for the pop band Maroon 5. He also lends his voice as a background singer. He is known for his unique artistry and studio work for other performers.\\n\\nA native of New Orleans, PJ was born into a lineage of gospel music, talent, and Christian leadership, to Bishop Paul Sylvester Morton and Dr. Debra Brown Morton. After graduating from St. Augustine High School, PJ went on to earn a degree in marketing from Morehouse College in Atlanta, Georgia. \\n\\nPJ contributed to India Arie's Grammy Award-winning album, \\\"Voyage to India,\\\" and he released his first album shortly after graduating college. The following year, he released his album, \\\"Gumbo,\u201d which included the Grammy Award-winning cover of the Bee Gees\u2019s, \\\"How Deep is Your Love.\\\" \\n\\nHe and his wife, Korti Lavoisier Ward was born June 14, 1959 in Starkville, MS. He was the middle child and only son to Walter and Betty Ward. He resided in Starkville, MS until 1962. He then moved to St. Louis, MO where he attended St. Matthews Catholic School until 6th Grade and then transferred to St. Rose of Lima Grade School where he was a member of the basketball team. He attended Mercy High School from 1973-1975 and later  transferred to Sumner High School where he was a member of the baseball team and graduated in May 1977. \\n\\nHe attended Central Missouri State University from 1977-1979 pursuing a degree in business and fashion design.  He returned to St Louis, MO and started his modeling career with several different agencies while working as the lead sales associate at Bachrach Men\u2019s Clothing Store in Frontenac Plaza located in Clayton, MO. This position lead to his personal shopper position that he maintained for 5 years before moving to Atlanta, GA where he became a manager, personal shopper and eventually a buyer for Alexander Julian. \\n\\nWhile working at Alexander Julian he was afforded the opportunity to become a partner and offered the opportunity to become the sole owner until he became ill and was no longer able to perform his duties. \\n\\nWalter always had a natural since for fashion and how to be unique and exquisitely dressed.  He frequently read fashion magazines such as GQ and other designer styles which had a huge influence on his dreams as a designer and fashion influencer. \\n\\nWalter died in May of 1991 before making that dream come to full fruition.  He left a sense of fashion on all of his family members and so many of his friends and clients who still wear some of his fashions today.  He truly made a mark on how fashions are and should be worn and no doubt would have been a well know entrepreneur.\",\"type\":1,\"created_at\":1666187189,\"created_at_utc\":1666187189,\"content_type\":\"comment\",\"status\":\"Active\",\"bit_flags\":0,\"did_report_as_spam\":false,\"share_enabled\":false,\"user\":{\"pk\":\"4339493993\",\"username\":\"lavoisiersuits\",\"full_name\":\"(Lava\u2022Seer)
